 SELECT MIN(a1.dep_time) FROM `ontime_mysiam`  AS a1 INNER JOIN `airports`  AS a2 ON KEYS [ a1.`origin` ] INNER JOIN `aircraft`  AS a3 ON KEYS [ a1.`tail_num`] WHERE   a1.`tail_num` LIKE 'N10%'  AND (  /*  .`manufacturer` LIKE 'N10%' */ 1 = 1  AND  /*  .`state_code` BETWEEN 'c' AND 'y' */ 1 = 1  AND   a2.`state` = 'NH'  AND  /*  .`name` LIKE 'N9Q%' */ 1 = 1  AND   a3.`state` BETWEEN 'g' AND 'v'  AND  /*  .`zipcode` BETWEEN 10000 + ( 29 * 100) AND 10000 + ( 85 * 100) */ 1 = 1  );
